posted:Posted June 1, 2024
msg:The room is not big but clean and tidy. The most important thing is that there is a dehumidifier working silently, so there is no odor in the room after sleeping for three days. The downside is that there are no plastic slippers for tourists to wear when taking a bath (you have to go to the supermarket to buy them at your own expense). The tea in the room is delicious, but unfortunately only four packs are available every day. A big advantage of this hotel is that it is close to the pier and the hotel has two or three medium-sized buses to pick up and drop off passengers between the hotel and the pier at any time. The fog closed the way on the morning of our departure from the island. Fortunately, the hotel sent a car to deliver our entrusted luggage to the pier in time, so that we could evacuate Putuoshan Island as soon as possible when navigation was restored. Perhaps this is the value of the high price of the hotel.

name:A‚Äçn‚Äço‚Äçn‚Äçy‚Äçm‚Äço‚Äçu‚Äçs‚Äç ‚ÄçU‚Äçs‚Äçe‚Äçr

posted:Posted March 26, 2024
msg:This was a very, very bad travel experience, never been so bad for the star rating booked on Trip.com (noted five stars).
This time, Trip.com also bears some responsibility for failing to clearly indicate the true condition of the hotel room when booking.
The very bad experience this time was: this five-star hotel actually arranged for us to stay in a room in the basement!
Except for the pick-up driver and the baggage guy, the service attitude of this hotel is good (we paid a tip), but the rest of the attitude is not good, especially the man who checked in, who had a poker face from beginning to end and checked himself for a long time. I couldn't find the reservation, so I questioned whether I had made a reservation! After telling him the reservation number, because I booked through Trip.com and my name uses Chinese pinyin, he asked with disdain why not use Chinese characters?
When the baggage boy took us to the room and told us that we had to go down 1 and a half floors (2 to 7 stairs, this building has no elevator and no barrier-free access), we almost collapsed. My brother and I both have bad legs. Walking on a flat road was okay, but it was very difficult to go up and down the stairs. After the luggage boy learned about this situation, he also took the initiative to contact the front desk via radio to see if he could adjust to a room on the first floor. The front desk replied that there were no rooms. But when my wife went to the front desk to argue, the front desk said that the room was available, but she had to pay extra. He also said that he originally had to pay more than 1,000 yuan, but because of the inconvenience of your feet, he charged more than 600 yuan.
This is not the first time we have stayed in a star-rated hotel. If the hotel has rooms, there is no problem in upgrading the room for free in this case. Unfortunately, we were unlucky and chose a so-called five-star hotel. It was a shady hotel that was only for profit in the name of a Buddhist resort. Even the basement was used as a room (there was no elevator).
In addition, there are more rooms in the basement, the rooms are small, and the design is also very poor. The sliding door of the toilet is connected to a small boiling water tank. When the toilet and bathroom are opened, the boiling water tank must be closed. When you come out of the toilet, your colleague is pouring water. , it was a very dangerous thing at that time. I opened the door and hit my wife. Fortunately, she reacted quickly, otherwise she would have suffered a bruise and swollen face.
The baggage boy deserves praise. We know he has no authority. But he offered to call when checking out and he would come over to help move the luggage.
It is recommended that Trip.com should indicate on the page that it is a basement room (I know I will definitely not book such a room)
There are many hotels in Putuo Mountain. If given the choice, no one would choose to stay in a hotel that is too popular.
